Iteganyagihe rirerire rivuga  nk'uko tuzagira imbeho yoroheje
Umwana muto wambaye ikoti ritukura na jans aryama mu rubura kugirango akore marayika wurubura
 Muri bisi nta bagenzi barenze batanu
amuhaye amafranga ye 
hari  igisimba zigomba kuba mu mashyamba
Hari icyo bakubwiye kuri gahunda zabo kuri uyu mugoroba? 
Tuzi  uko kumenya Imana bishingiye ku buryo yaganiraga
Nkuko nabikubwiye mbere ntabwo nteganya kuzaba mu nama ya nyuma ya saa sita.
